Brazil's leader, the Vice President, Luiz Inácio Lula da Silva, has been named the most powerful man in the world. His country's economy is booming and he has become a leading voice for the world's poor. The World Economic Forum, which compiles the list, says the President's power has increased because of his leadership during the recent financial crisis.  The US President, George W. Bush, is ranked second on the list, followed by Russian Prime Minister Vladimir Putin. The list also includes British Prime Minister Gordon Brown, Indian Prime Minister Manmohan Singh, and Chinese President Hu Jintao.  The top ten is completed by French President Nicolas Sarkozy, German Chancellor Angela Merkel, and Spanish Prime Minister José Luis Rodríguez Zapatero.  The list is based on a survey of leading business people and experts. It is compiled annually and is based on a range of factors including political and economic influence, media exposure, and leadership ability.  The list is published as part of a report which also looks at the current economic climate and the future of global leadership.  The World Economic Forum is an independent international organization that works to improve the state of the world by engaging business, politics, academic and other leaders of society to shape global, regional and industry agendas.  It is based in Geneva, Switzerland, and is funded by private sector donors.  The Forum has a membership of over 1,000 corporate leaders and 2,000 experts from more than 80 countries. It also has a growing network of partners.  The Forum's mission is to improve the state of the world by engaging business, political, academic and other leaders of society to shape global, regional and industry agendas. It does so by convening stakeholders, undertaking research, disseminating knowledge and providing policy recommendations.  The Forum's top priorities are the growing global economic crisis and the deteriorating state of the environment.  The Forum's work is organized around three core activities:  * Conferences - The Forum convenes business, political, academic and other leaders to shape global, regional and industry agendas.  * Public Policy - The Forum provides research, policy recommendations and tools to governments, corporations and civil society.  * Knowledge - The Forum disseminates knowledge and builds networks to help leaders understand and respond to the global economy and society.  The Forum is independent of governments and institutions

It is located in the north of the city, bordering the town of San Sebastián de los Reyes and the city of Madrid. It is located 15 kilometres north of Madrid. The Quine Tapes was a bootleg series of albums released by Polydor Records. The series was originally released in the UK by Polydor Records in the 1970s, but was later re-released in the United States by Universal Music Group. The albums were originally released by Polydor Records and distributed by EMI Music. The original release of the series was not authorized by the artist and was later withdrawn from sale. The series was re-released in the United States in 1996, under Universal Music Group, with different cover art, but the same tracks. The series was released in the UK in 1971, in a period when the band was not signed to a major label, and therefore was not authorized by the band. The series was not officially released in the United States until 1996, under Universal Music Group, with the same tracks as the original series. The series is now out of print. Buzz Aldrin was the second man to walk on the Moon, on the Apollo 11 mission in 1969. He was born in Chicago in 1930 and graduated from MIT in 1963 with a degree in Aerospace Engineering. He was the first to set foot on the lunar surface. He was also the first to step off the lunar surface and into space, by ascending into the Lunar Module piloted by Neil Armstrong, and the first to step back onto the Moon's surface. He was also the first person to ride in the Lunar Module during the flight to the Moon. He was the pilot of the Lunar Module during the lunar landing and the lunar ascent. He was the commander of the Apollo 11 mission. He is now a businessman, and lives in Florida.

The Quine Tapes is a bootleg series of The Velvet Underground's first two albums. The series was released in 1973 by Flair Records in the U.K. and by New York-based label Stiff Records in the U.S. The albums were originally released by the band's manager, Andy Warhol, in 1967, and are known as The Velvet Underground & Nico and The Velvet Underground. The series of bootleg recordings was made by a group of students who attended a gig in San Francisco, in the summer of 1967. The group was the Quine family, and the tapes were originally recorded for the purpose of listening to them at home. The Quine Tapes is a rock music album. The Quine Tapes is preceded by Squeeze (The Velvet Underground album). The Quine Tapes was recorded in San Francisco.

Bondareva, Olga Nikolaevna (1937-), Russian mathematician, born in Leningrad. She received her Ph.D. in 1966 from Leningrad State University, where she was a student of Vladimir Arnold. She is known for her work in the theory of dynamical systems, specifically the study of Hamiltonian systems and symplectic geometry. In 1975 she proved with Edward W. Shapley the theorem that is named after them, which gives a criterion for the existence of a Lagrangian submanifold of a symplectic manifold.

The Estádio Municipal Coaracy da Mata Fonseca is a football stadium in Arapiraca, state of Alagoas, Brazil. It is currently used mostly for football matches, but also for other events such as shows and religious events. It is the home ground of ASA.  ASA is a football club based in Arapiraca. It currently plays in the Campeonato Brasileiro Série C, the third division of the Brazilian football league system. The club was founded in 1947 and is the most successful football club in Alagoas, with the most titles won in the state. It has won the Alagoano Championship eight times, the Copa Alagoas four times and the Copa dos Campeões Alagoanos four times. It has also won the Campeonato Brasileiro Série D twice, in 2006 and 2008.  ASA has 17,000 members.  ASA's home ground is the Estádio Municipal Coaracy da Mata Fonseca.  ASA's full name is "Agremiação Sportiva Arapiraquense".  ASA won the Campeonato Brasileiro Série C in 2015, defeating Vila Nova Football Club in the final.  ASA is part of the Campeonato Brasileiro Série C 2015.

Roadburn Festival, the annual post-rock festival in the Netherlands, is proud to announce that Year of No Light, the hardcore band from Tulsa, Oklahoma, will be performing at Roadburn 2008. They will be playing a showcase with the festival’s new label, Roadburn Records. Year of No Light’s debut album, Year of No Light, was produced by Roadburn Festival founder, John Porter, and was released in May 2007 on Ipecac Recordings. The album was the first release on Roadburn Records, the label started by John Porter and the Roadburn Festival team to release the festival’s own line-up and new bands.

The City Manager of Ciudad Ayala is an elected position with a four-year term of office. The City Manager is the chief administrative officer of the City and is responsible for the administration of all City departments, except police and fire departments. The City Manager is also responsible for the financial management of the City. The City Manager is responsible for submitting a comprehensive annual budget to the City Council. The City Manager is responsible for submitting an annual report to the City Council. The City Manager is responsible for the administration of the City's public works department, the administration of the City's public utilities department, and the administration of the City's housing department.

The Quine Tapes is a bootleg series of The Velvet Underground's first two albums Squeeze (1967) and White Light/White Heat (1968). The series was released by Polydor Records and recorded in San Francisco.  Bootleg Series Volume 1: The Quine Tapes is a compilation of live recordings of The Velvet Underground that were recorded during their first two US tours and released in the UK by Polydor Records in 1975. The album is noteworthy for its inclusion of a number of previously unreleased performances, including early versions of several songs from The Velvet Underground & Nico, as well as the live debut of the Velvets' song "Sunday Morning".  The album's title refers to the name of the tape recorder used to record the performances. In a 2007 interview, the band's original guitarist Sterling Morrison explained that the name was a reference to the large number of times the tape recorder would break down during the band's performances.  Bootleg Series Volume 1: The Quine Tapes was released in the UK in 1975 by Polydor Records and distributed by WEA Records. The album was reissued in the US in 1992 by Rhino Records. In 2004, the album was reissued on CD by Rhino Records with the addition of five previously unreleased tracks.
Bun an Chéad Thiar na hÉireann is a city in the province of Valencia, Spain. It is located in the Serranía de Cuenca, in the centre of the Iberian Peninsula. The city is the capital of the comarca of La Serranía. The population of the municipality is 3,983, and the population of the city itself is 3,470. The city is located in the north-eastern part of the Serranía de Cuenca. It is situated in a mountainous area, with an average altitude of 1,150 metres (3,970 ft) above sea level. It is surrounded by a number of mountains, including the Pico del Buitre, the Pico de la Cruz, the Cerro de la Cruz, the Cerro de San Cristóbal, and the Cerro de San Pedro. The city was founded in the 14th century, and is named after a native of the city, Juan Nolasco.

The Estádio Municipal Coaracy da Mata Fonseca is a football stadium in Arapiraca, Alagoas. It is the home ground of Agremiação Sportiva Arapiraquense. It was inaugurated on November 29, 2005, and has a maximum capacity of 12,000 people. It is currently used mainly for association football, and hosted the 2015 Campeonato Brasileiro Série C.  The Agremiação Sportiva Arapiraquense, also known as ASA, is a football club from Arapiraca, Alagoas. It was founded on June 14, 1928. It currently plays in the Campeonato Brasileiro Série C.  The 2015 Campeonato Brasileiro Série C was the fifth season of the Campeonato Brasileiro Série C, the third level of the Brazilian football league system. It was won by Vila Nova Futebol Clube. Na Hypermarcas, Glenn Greenwald publicou uma história em que disse que a empresa estava pagando propina ao então governador de Minas Gerais, Eduardo Azeredo, para vencer a licitação para instalar um sistema de bilhetagem eletrônica no Estado. O jornalista afirma que os pagamentos teriam sido feitos através de uma conta em Liechtenstein, que teria sido aberta por Marcos Valério, operador do mensalão. O caso, segundo Greenwald, foi revelado pelo ex-diretor da empresa, Ricardo Pernambuco, que está preso na penitenciária de Tremembé, no interior de São Paulo. A defesa da empresa afirmou que não há provas do envolvimento da empresa no caso e que o ex-diretor foi demitido por ter fraudado documentos. A Hypermarcas é um dos maiores grupos do setor de bens de consumo do Brasil, com faturamento anual de R$ 12,5 bilhões. A empresa é dona de marcas como Omo, Minuano e Bozzano. Fundada em 2001 por João Alves de Queiroz Filho, a Hypermarcas é a terceira maior empresa do setor de higiene e beleza do país. Queiroz Filho é filho de João Alves de Queiroz, um dos maiores empresários do setor de combustíveis do país. Queiroz Filho também é sócio do Banco Bozano Simonsen. O banco, que também é controlado por Queiroz, foi um dos principais responsáveis pelo financiamento de campanhas eleitorais no país. O Bozano Simonsen é sócio do Banco Pactual, um dos principais bancos de investimentos do país. O Pactual é controlado por André Esteves, que também é sócio da corretora de valores BTG Pactual, que está sendo investigada por ter sido utilizada para o pagamento de propina ao PT durante o governo Lula. A Hypermarcas possui mais de 1.400 produtos, entre medicamentos, produtos de higiene pessoal, beleza e limpeza, e está presente em todos os estados brasileiros. A empresa possui um centro de distribuição em São Paulo, uma fábrica de medicamentos em Hortolândia, no interior do estado, e uma fábrica de produtos de higiene em Anápolis, no interior de Goiás. A empresa também possui um centro de distribuição em Santa Catarina, uma fábrica de produtos de beleza em Manaus, no Amazonas, e uma fábrica de produtos de limpeza em Feira de Santana, na Bahia.
